\DoxyCodeLine{1527 \textcolor{comment}{ * The last semantic modification to khrplatform.h was at commit ID:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1528 \textcolor{comment}{ *      67a3e0864c2d75ea5287b9f3d2eb74a745936692}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1529 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1530 \textcolor{comment}{ * Adopters may modify this file to suit their platform. Adopters are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1531 \textcolor{comment}{ * encouraged to submit platform specific modifications to the Khronos}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1532 \textcolor{comment}{ * group so that they can be included in future versions of this file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1533 \textcolor{comment}{ * Please submit changes by filing pull requests or issues on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1534 \textcolor{comment}{ * the EGL Registry repository linked above.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1535 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1536 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1537 \textcolor{comment}{ * See the Implementer's Guidelines for information about where this file}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1538 \textcolor{comment}{ * should be located on your system and for more details of its use:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1539 \textcolor{comment}{ *    http://www.khronos.org/registry/implementers\_guide.pdf}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1540 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1541 \textcolor{comment}{ * This file should be included as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1542 \textcolor{comment}{ *        \#include <KHR/khrplatform.h>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1543 \textcolor{comment}{ * by Khronos client API header files that use its types and defines.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1544 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1545 \textcolor{comment}{ * The types in khrplatform.h should only be used to define API-\/specific types.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1546 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1547 \textcolor{comment}{ * Types defined in khrplatform.h:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1548 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_int8\_t              signed   8  bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1549 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_uint8\_t             unsigned 8  bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1550 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_int16\_t             signed   16 bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1551 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_uint16\_t            unsigned 16 bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1552 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_int32\_t             signed   32 bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1553 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_uint32\_t            unsigned 32 bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1554 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_int64\_t             signed   64 bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1555 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_uint64\_t            unsigned 64 bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1556 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_intptr\_t            signed   same number of bits as a pointer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1557 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_uintptr\_t           unsigned same number of bits as a pointer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1558 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_ssize\_t             signed   size}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1559 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_usize\_t             unsigned size}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1560 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_float\_t             signed   32 bit floating point}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1561 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_time\_ns\_t           unsigned 64 bit time in nanoseconds}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1562 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_utime\_nanoseconds\_t unsigned time interval or absolute time in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1563 \textcolor{comment}{ *                                         nanoseconds}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1564 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_stime\_nanoseconds\_t signed time interval in nanoseconds}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1565 \textcolor{comment}{ *    khronos\_boolean\_enum\_t      enumerated boolean type. This should}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1566 \textcolor{comment}{ *      only be used as a base type when a client API's boolean type is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1567 \textcolor{comment}{ *      an enum. Client APIs which use an integer or other type for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1568 \textcolor{comment}{ *      booleans cannot use this as the base type for their boolean.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1569 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1570 \textcolor{comment}{ * Tokens defined in khrplatform.h:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1571 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1572 \textcolor{comment}{ *    KHRONOS\_FALSE, KHRONOS\_TRUE Enumerated boolean false/true values.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1573 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1574 \textcolor{comment}{ *    KHRONOS\_SUPPORT\_INT64 is 1 if 64 bit integers are supported; otherwise 0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1575 \textcolor{comment}{ *    KHRONOS\_SUPPORT\_FLOAT is 1 if floats are supported; otherwise 0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1576 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1577 \textcolor{comment}{ * Calling convention macros defined in this file:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1578 \textcolor{comment}{ *    KHRONOS\_APICALL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1579 \textcolor{comment}{ *    KHRONOS\_GLAD\_API\_PTR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1580 \textcolor{comment}{ *    KHRONOS\_APIATTRIBUTES}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1581 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1582 \textcolor{comment}{ * These may be used in function prototypes as:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1583 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1584 \textcolor{comment}{ *      KHRONOS\_APICALL void KHRONOS\_GLAD\_API\_PTR funcname(}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1585 \textcolor{comment}{ *                                  int arg1,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1586 \textcolor{comment}{ *                                  int arg2) KHRONOS\_APIATTRIBUTES;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1587 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1588 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1589 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(\_\_SCITECH\_SNAP\_\_) \&\& !defined(KHRONOS\_STATIC)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1753 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if KHRONOS\_SUPPORT\_INT64}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1754 \textcolor{comment}{/* Time types}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1755 \textcolor{comment}{ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1756 \textcolor{comment}{ * These types can be used to represent a time interval in nanoseconds or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1757 \textcolor{comment}{ * an absolute Unadjusted System Time.  Unadjusted System Time is the number}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1758 \textcolor{comment}{ * of nanoseconds since some arbitrary system event (e.g. since the last}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1759 \textcolor{comment}{ * time the system booted).  The Unadjusted System Time is an unsigned}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1760 \textcolor{comment}{ * 64 bit value that wraps back to 0 every 584 years.  Time intervals}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1761 \textcolor{comment}{ * may be either signed or unsigned.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1762 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1763 \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} khronos\_uint64\_t       khronos\_utime\_nanoseconds\_t;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1764 \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} khronos\_int64\_t        khronos\_stime\_nanoseconds\_t;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1765 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1766 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1767 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1768 \textcolor{comment}{ * Dummy value used to pad enum types to 32 bits.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1769 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1770 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef KHRONOS\_MAX\_ENUM}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1771 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define KHRONOS\_MAX\_ENUM 0x7FFFFFFF}}
